\index{x509\+Get\+Sign\+Hash\+Algo@{x509\+Get\+Sign\+Hash\+Algo}!certificate/x509\+\_\+common.\+h@{certificate/x509\+\_\+common.\+h}}
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{x509\+Get\+Sign\+Hash\+Algo()}{x509GetSignHashAlgo()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \hyperlink{error_8h_ac7659d73a8cdedc08e9f566bb406689c}{error\+\_\+t} x509\+Get\+Sign\+Hash\+Algo (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \hyperlink{structX509SignatureAlgoId}{X509\+Signature\+Algo\+Id} $\ast$}]{sign\+Algo\+Id,  }\item[{\hyperlink{certificate_2x509__common_8h_ac7f323ef3436e8cc3a89862a5e818078}{X509\+Signature\+Algo} $\ast$}]{sign\+Algo,  }\item[{const \hyperlink{structHashAlgo}{Hash\+Algo} $\ast$$\ast$}]{hash\+Algo }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Get the signature and hash algorithms that match the specified identifier. 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em sign\+Algo\+Id} & Signature algorithm identifier \\
\hline

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \hyperlink{compiler__port_8h_a812d16e5494522586b3784e55d479912}{bool\+\_\+t} x509\+Is\+Hash\+Algo\+Supported (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\hyperlink{certificate_2x509__common_8h_a6a9d4c3832120bb78c1ac7117bfbdf06}{X509\+Hash\+Algo}}]{hash\+Algo }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}
